–°–µ—Ä–≥—ñ–π –ú.: –≤–æ—Ç —Ç–µ–±–µ

–°–µ—Ä–≥—ñ–π –ú.: 100% ‚Äî FF 95% ‚Äî F2 90% ‚Äî E6 85% ‚Äî D9 80% ‚Äî CC 75% ‚Äî BF 70% ‚Äî B3 65% ‚Äî A6 60% ‚Äî 99 55% ‚Äî 8C 50% ‚Äî 80 45% ‚Äî 73 40% ‚Äî 66 35% ‚Äî 59 30% ‚Äî 4D 25% ‚Äî 40 20% ‚Äî 33 15% ‚Äî 26 10% ‚Äî 1A 5% ‚Äî 0D 0% ‚Äî 00 Put those codes at the end of the hexcode for the background color:  Ex: I want to get a black background with 70% opacity, I use the hex code for black (#000000) and add B3 to the end: #000000B3
